<script type="text/javascript">
	var _szUserId = '';
	var isLogin = 0;
	var adPlayer = null;	// 메인 슬라이딩 광고 TI 영상 플레이어 변수

	// 창크기 변환 리스트
	$(window).ready(function(){
		function adjustSize(width) {
			if (width > 1) {
				$('div#wideArea').attr('class', 'content_area');
			}
			if (width > 1493) {
				$('div#wideArea').attr('class', 'content_area listfive');
			}
			if (width > 1737) {
				$('div#wideArea').attr('class', 'content_area listsix');
			}
		}

		$(function() {
			adjustSize($(this).width());
			$(window).resize(function() {
				adjustSize($(this).width());
			});

			// 광고tag주소 국내/해외 설정
			szAdTagUrl = '//pa.afreecatv.com/RealMedia/ads/adstream_sx.ads/pc.web.in/banner/main@Top1?mid_id=afreecaAd&aftvlid=';
			if (szLang != "ko_KR"){
				szAdTagUrl = '//pa.afreecatv.com/RealMedia/ads/adstream_sx.ads/pc.webg.in/banner/main@Top1?mid_id=afreecaAd&aftvlid=';
			}
			if ((checkSimple("main","ad_banner")) && (_szCurHash =="" || _szCurHash == "all") && 1)
			{
				$.getScript(szAdTagUrl, function () {
					try {
						// 광고 영상 URL 있을 경우에만 광고 플레이어 호출함
						if (typeof szVodUrl != "undefined") {
							$('head').append( $('<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css"/>').attr('href', '//res-cf.afreecatv.com/css/global/afreecatv_player/afreecatv_player.css') );
							$.ajax({
								dataType: 'script',
								cache: true,
								url: '//static-cf.afreecatv.com/asset/app/adplayer/AdPlayer.min.js'
							});
						}
					} catch(e) { }
				});
			}
		});
	});

	require.config({
		urlArgs: '' //'v=' + (+new Date())//AppVersion
		, paths: {
			favorite : 'app/main/favorite.global'
            , recent : 'app/main/recent'
			, search : 'app/main/search.global'
			, hashtag : 'app/main/hashtag.global'
			, doT :	'app/main/doT.min'
			, view : 'app/main/view.global.broadlist'
			, banner : 'app/main/banner.category'
			, bxSlider : '//res-cf.afreecatv.com/script/common/jquery.bxslider.4.1.2.min'
			, mousewheel : '//res-cf.afreecatv.com/script/afmain/jquery.mousewheel.min'
			, mCustomScrollbar : '//res-cf.afreecatv.com/script/afmain/jquery.mCustomScrollbar.concat.min'
		}
		, shim: {
			'bxSlider' : {
				deps: ['jquery']

				deps: ['jquery']

			}

		, callback: function() {
			requirejs(['app'], function(app) {
				app.start();
			}, function(err) {
			});
		}
	});

	define('preLoad', ['afreeca', 'bxSlider'], function() {
	});

	var _search;
	define('app', ['afreeca', 'view', 'search', 'preLoad','mCustomScrollbar'], function(afreeca, view, search) {

if(document.getElementById("noticeScroll")){
	var scrollup = new ScrollText("noticeScroll");
	scrollup.LineHeight = 24;        //单排文字滚动的高度
	scrollup.Amount = 1;            //注意:子模块(LineHeight)一定要能整除Amount.
	scrollup.Delay = 20;           //延时
	scrollup.Start();             //文字自动滚动
	scrollup.Direction = "up";   //默认设置为文字向上滚动
}		
$(function(){
	$(window).on('scroll',function(){
		var st = $(document).scrollTop();
		if( st>0 ){
			if( $('#content').length != 0  ){
				var w = $(window).width(),mw = $('#content').width();
				if( (w-mw)/2 > 70 )
					$('#gotop').css({'left':(w-mw)/2+mw+20});
				else{
					$('#gotop').css({'left':'auto'});
				}
			}
			$('#gotop').fadeIn(function(){
				$(this).removeClass('hide');
			});
		}else{
			$('#gotop').fadeOut(function(){
				$(this).addClass('hide');
			});
		}	
	});
	$('#gotop .go').on('click',function(){
		$('html,body').animate({'scrollTop':0},500);
	});

	$('#gotop .cz-weixin').hover(function(){
		$('#gotop .cz-weixin-con').removeClass('hide');
	},function(){
		$('#gotop .cz-weixin-con').addClass('hide');
	});
});

	</script>

					});

    <script type="text/javascript">
        var sendPageLoadEvent = function () {
            setTimeout(function () {
                var timing = window.performance.timing;
                var hepsiBus = window['hepsiBus'];
                if (!!hepsiBus && timing) {
                    hepsiBus.track('PageLoad',
                    {
                        domLoaded: (timing.domContentLoadedEventEnd - timing.navigationStart) / 1000,
                        ready: (timing.loadEventEnd - timing.navigationStart) / 1000,
                        experiments: hepsiBus.parsers ? hepsiBus.parsers.getExperiments() : [],
                        page: !!window['utagObject'] ? window['utagObject'].page_name : ''
                    });
                }
            }, 0);
        };

        window.addEventListener('load', sendPageLoadEvent, false);
    </script>
